      function alerts_ShowUnSubscribeeTOCPopup(title, alertType, journalId) {
         var unSubscribeeTocPopup = $find('unSubscribeToAlerts');
         var lblUnsubscribeMessage = document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_lblUnsubscribeMessage');
         lblUnsubscribeMessage.innerHTML = title;
         document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenUnSubscribeAlertType').value = alertType;
         document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenUnsubscribeMessage').value = title;
 
         $('#' + 'ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_pUnsubscribeButtons').show();
 
         if (document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenJournalId').value == null || document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenJournalId').value == '') {
             document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_ucUnsubscribeToAlertsUserControl_hiddenJournalId').value = journalId;
         }
 
         if (unSubscribeeTocPopup != null) {
             unSubscribeeTocPopup.show();
         }
     }

     <script type="text/javascript">
      function alerts_SaveSubscriptionTypeInHiddenField(url, subscriptionType, journalId) {
         $('#' + 'ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_SubscribeToEtocPopupControl_hiddenSubscriptionType').val(subscriptionType);
         $('#' + 'ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_SubscribeToEtocPopupControl_hiddenJournalId').val(journalId);
         if (url)
             window.location = url;
         else 
             __doPostBack('hypSubscribeToAlerts');
         return false;
     }
 
     function alerts_ShowSubscribeeTOCPopup(journalTitle, journalId) {
         var subscribeToEtocPopup = $find('subscribeToEtoc');
         subscribeToEtocPopup.show();
         var modelPopupState = document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_SubscribeToEtocPopupControl_hiddenSubscribeToEtocPopupState');
         var emailTextBox = document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_SubscribeToEtocPopupControl_txtEmailAddress');
         var thanksPanel = document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_SubscribeToEtocPopupControl_pnlAuthenticatedUser');
         var mainPanel = document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_SubscribeToEtocPopupControl_pnlMain');
         var thankYouMessageUnAuthenticated = document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_SubscribeToEtocPopupControl_lblThankYouMessage');
         var thankYouMessageAuthenticated = document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_SubscribeToEtocPopupControl_lblAuthenticatedUserTitle');
 
         if (modelPopupState.value == 'showthanksmessage') {
             thanksPanel.style.display = "block";
             mainPanel.style.display = "none";
             thankYouMessageAuthenticated.innerHTML = "Thank you for subscribing to the eTOC for " + journalTitle + ".";
         }
 
         if (modelPopupState.value == 'showemail') {
             thanksPanel.style.display = "none";
             mainPanel.style.display = "block";
             thankYouMessageUnAuthenticated.innerHTML = "Thank you for choosing to subscribe to the eTOC for " + journalTitle + ".";
         }
 
         if ($('.etoc-popup') != null) {
             document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_SubscribeToEtocPopupControl_hiddenJournalId').value = journalId;
 
             if (modelPopupState.value == 'showemail')
                 emailTextBox.focus();
         }
     }
 
     $('.js-close').click(function () {
         var pageUrl = document.getElementById('ctl00_ucUserActionsToolbar_SubscribeToEtocPopupControl_hiddenConfirmSubscriptionPageUrl');
         var subscribeeTocPopup = $find('subscribeToEtoc');
         if (subscribeeTocPopup != null) {
             subscribeeTocPopup.hide();
             if (pageUrl.value !== '' && pageUrl.value !== window.location.pathname)
                 window.location = pageUrl.value;
         }
         return false;
     });
     </script>

     <script>
      $(function () {
         //find recent searches link and move container
         var recentSearchesControl = $("a[id$='RecentSearches']");
         if (recentSearchesControl.length) {
             $("#ResentSearchContainer").appendTo(recentSearchesControl.parent());
             recentSearchesControl.click(function(e) {
                 e.stopPropagation();
 
                 if ($("#ResentSearchContainer").is(":hidden")) {
                     $("#ResentSearchContainer").slideDown("slow");
                     recentSearchesControl.addClass('open');
                 } else {
                     $("#ResentSearchContainer").hide();
                     recentSearchesControl.removeClass('open');
                 }
             });
         }
         //move journal administration link to current active account menu
         if ($("a[id$='hypAdministration']").length)
             $("<li>").append($("a[id$='hypAdministration']")).appendTo($(".user-info-dropdown"));
 
         var eTocAccountLink = $("ul.user-info-dropdown>li>a[id='SubscribeToEToc']");
         if (eTocAccountLink.length) {
             eTocAccountLink.parent().html($("#eTocTop>a"));
         }
     });
     </script>

             <script type="text/javascript">
              var atmcDescription;
     var atmcCollectionName;
     var atmcRdoExistingCollection;
     var atmcRdoExistingCollectionChecked;
     var atmcRdoNewCollection;
     function atmcGetPopup() { return $find('addToMyCollectionsPopupExtender__1867194667'); }
     var atmcPnlMain;
     var atmcPnlMessage;
     var atmcCmbExistingCollection;
     var atmcParaCollectionName;
     var atmcParaCollectionDescription;
     var atmcCustomValidator;
 
     $(document).ready(function () {
         atmc_InitializeControls();
     });
 
     function atmc_attachFocusHandler() {
         if (atmcPnlMain != null && atmcPnlMain.style.display != 'none' && atmcGetPopup() != null) {
             atmcGetPopup().add_shown(atmc_SetFocusOnControl);
         }
     }
 
     function atmc_InitializeControls() {
         atmcDescription = $get('ctl00_ctl46_g_52b82c2c_94e4_4f1c_a3f0_eb717625adfe_ctl00_txtDescription');
         atmcCollectionName = $get('ctl00_ctl46_g_52b82c2c_94e4_4f1c_a3f0_eb717625adfe_ctl00_txtCollectionName');
         atmcRdoExistingCollection = $get('ctl00_ctl46_g_52b82c2c_94e4_4f1c_a3f0_eb717625adfe_ctl00_rdoExistingCollection');
         atmcRdoExistingCollectionChecked = false;
         atmcRdoNewCollection = $get('ctl00_ctl46_g_52b82c2c_94e4_4f1c_a3f0_eb717625adfe_ctl00_rdoNewCollection');
         atmcPnlMain = $get('ctl00_ctl46_g_52b82c2c_94e4_4f1c_a3f0_eb717625adfe_ctl00_pnlMain');
         atmcPnlMessage = $get('ctl00_ctl46_g_52b82c2c_94e4_4f1c_a3f0_eb717625adfe_ctl00_pnlMessage');
         atmcCmbExistingCollection = $get('ctl00_ctl46_g_52b82c2c_94e4_4f1c_a3f0_eb717625adfe_ctl00_cmbExistingCollection');
         atmcParaCollectionName = $get('paraCollectionName');
         atmcParaCollectionDescription = $get('paraCollectionDescription');
         atmcCustomValidator = $get('ctl00_ctl46_g_52b82c2c_94e4_4f1c_a3f0_eb717625adfe_ctl00_customValidator');
 
         atmcCollectionName.disabled = atmcRdoExistingCollectionChecked;
         atmcDescription.disabled = atmcRdoExistingCollectionChecked;
     }
 
     function atmc_SetFocusOnControl() {
 
         if (atmcCustomValidator != null && atmcCustomValidator.style.display != 'none') {
             atmcRdoNewCollection.checked = true;
             atmcCollectionName.disabled = false;
             atmcDescription.disabled = false;
             atmcParaCollectionName.className = "";
             atmcParaCollectionDescription.className = "";
             atmcCmbExistingCollection.disabled = true;
             atmcCollectionName.focus();
             atmcCollectionName.select();
         }
         atmcSetFocus();
     }
 
     Sys.WebForms.PageRequestManager.getInstance().add_pageLoaded(atmc_attachFocusHandler);
     //Document.Ready() does not work after postback.This is a problem with partial postback.
     //The DOM isn't reloaded and so the document ready function won't be hit again. In order 
     //to achieve such functionality we need to assign a partial postback handler.
     Sys.WebForms.PageRequestManager.getInstance().add_pageLoaded(atmc_InitializeControls);
             </script>

             <script type="text/javascript">
              var atmcDescription;
     var atmcCollectionName;
     var atmcRdoExistingCollection;
     var atmcRdoExistingCollectionChecked;
     var atmcRdoNewCollection;
     function atmcGetPopup() { return $find('addToMyCollectionsPopupExtender__1833305023'); }
     var atmcPnlMain;
     var atmcPnlMessage;
     var atmcCmbExistingCollection;
     var atmcParaCollectionName;
     var atmcParaCollectionDescription;
     var atmcCustomValidator;
 
     $(document).ready(function () {
         atmc_InitializeControls();
     });
 
     function atmc_attachFocusHandler() {
         if (atmcPnlMain != null && atmcPnlMain.style.display != 'none' && atmcGetPopup() != null) {
             atmcGetPopup().add_shown(atmc_SetFocusOnControl);
         }
     }
 
     function atmc_InitializeControls() {
         atmcDescription = $get('ctl00_ctl46_g_cc2597fe_c296_4667_9005_f0d3f72f781a_ctl00_txtDescription');
         atmcCollectionName = $get('ctl00_ctl46_g_cc2597fe_c296_4667_9005_f0d3f72f781a_ctl00_txtCollectionName');
         atmcRdoExistingCollection = $get('ctl00_ctl46_g_cc2597fe_c296_4667_9005_f0d3f72f781a_ctl00_rdoExistingCollection');
         atmcRdoExistingCollectionChecked = false;
         atmcRdoNewCollection = $get('ctl00_ctl46_g_cc2597fe_c296_4667_9005_f0d3f72f781a_ctl00_rdoNewCollection');
         atmcPnlMain = $get('ctl00_ctl46_g_cc2597fe_c296_4667_9005_f0d3f72f781a_ctl00_pnlMain');
         atmcPnlMessage = $get('ctl00_ctl46_g_cc2597fe_c296_4667_9005_f0d3f72f781a_ctl00_pnlMessage');
         atmcCmbExistingCollection = $get('ctl00_ctl46_g_cc2597fe_c296_4667_9005_f0d3f72f781a_ctl00_cmbExistingCollection');
         atmcParaCollectionName = $get('paraCollectionName');
         atmcParaCollectionDescription = $get('paraCollectionDescription');
         atmcCustomValidator = $get('ctl00_ctl46_g_cc2597fe_c296_4667_9005_f0d3f72f781a_ctl00_customValidator');
 
         atmcCollectionName.disabled = atmcRdoExistingCollectionChecked;
         atmcDescription.disabled = atmcRdoExistingCollectionChecked;
     }
 
     function atmc_SetFocusOnControl() {
 
         if (atmcCustomValidator != null && atmcCustomValidator.style.display != 'none') {
             atmcRdoNewCollection.checked = true;
             atmcCollectionName.disabled = false;
             atmcDescription.disabled = false;
             atmcParaCollectionName.className = "";
             atmcParaCollectionDescription.className = "";
             atmcCmbExistingCollection.disabled = true;
             atmcCollectionName.focus();
             atmcCollectionName.select();
         }
         atmcSetFocus();
     }
 
     Sys.WebForms.PageRequestManager.getInstance().add_pageLoaded(atmc_attachFocusHandler);
     //Document.Ready() does not work after postback.This is a problem with partial postback.
     //The DOM isn't reloaded and so the document ready function won't be hit again. In order 
     //to achieve such functionality we need to assign a partial postback handler.
     Sys.WebForms.PageRequestManager.getInstance().add_pageLoaded(atmc_InitializeControls);

              <header>
               <h2 aria-expanded="false">
                Annual Meeting
               </h2>
              </header>
              <div class="content-box-body html-contents">
               <p>
                <strong>
                 21st Annual Meeting of the International Society for ECT and Neurostimulation (formerly the ACT)
                </strong>
               </p>
               <p>
                <strong>
                </strong>
                The 2011 Annual Meeting of the International Society for Neurostimulation will be held on Sunday, May 15th,at the annual meeting of the American Psychiatric Association (APA).
               </p>
               <p>
                To become a member of the ISEN, please complete the
                <a href="http://www.act-ect.org/?q=node/936" target="_blank" title="">
                 Membership Application
                </a>
                located on the ISEN's website.
               </p>
              </div>

             <script>
              $(function () {
         // Handles tab click
         $('ul[role="tablist"] > li').click(function () {
             // Get current tab
             var element = $(this);
 
             // Add loading icon
             element.children('a').children('i').show();
 
             // Swap active class
             $('ul[role="tablist"] > li').removeClass('active');
             element.addClass('active');
 
             // Post button click to server via ajax update panel
             var source = element.attr('aria-controls');
             switch (source) {
                 case 'MostViewed':
                     document.getElementById('ctl00_ctl46_g_f3503865_b3ea_4bc7_b6eb_70290260689b_ctl00_mostViewedLinkButton').click();
                     break;
                 case 'MostEmailed':
                     document.getElementById('ctl00_ctl46_g_f3503865_b3ea_4bc7_b6eb_70290260689b_ctl00_mostEmailedLinkButton').click();
                     break;
                 case 'HighestImpact':
                     document.getElementById('ctl00_ctl46_g_f3503865_b3ea_4bc7_b6eb_70290260689b_ctl00_highImpactedLinkButton').click();
                     break;
             }
 
         });
     });
 
     // Update Panel page load
     function pageLoad(sender, args) {
         // Reset loading state
         $('ul[role="tablist"] > li > a> i').hide();
     }
             </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    try {
 
         var adConfig = {
             "pageType": "home",
             "pageTargeting": {
                 "AccountId": "",
                 "Profession": "",
                 "Speciality": "",
                 "Country": "",
                 "Zip": "",
                 "UserSubcriptions": "",
                 "Institution": "",
                 "TopTenJournals": "ectjournal"
             },
             "pdata": {
                 "pubId": "113",
                 "siteId": "11301",
                 "pl": "5188",
                 "cid": "",
                 "url": "//services.journals.lww.com/IntegrationServices/AdService.svc/GetAds"
             },
             "slotClass": "ad-slot-container",
             "topBanner": {
                 "sticky": true,
                 "stickyDuration": Number(5000)
             }
         };
 
         var pageType = adConfig.pageType;
 
         var collectionName = '';
         var collectionId = '';
         var AccessionNumber = '';
 
         function SetAdditionalTargetting() {
             if (adConfig.pageType === "collections") {
                 adConfig.pageTargeting["CollectionId"] = "0";
                 adConfig.pageTargeting["CollectionName"] = "";
             }
 
             if (adConfig.pageType === "article") {
                 adConfig.pageTargeting["ArticleId"] = "";
 
 
                 
                 var collections = [];
 
                 if (collections.length) {
                     adConfig.pageTargeting["CollectionId"] = collections;
                 }
             }
 
             if (adConfig.pageType === "other") {
                 var landingPageType = 'pages'.toLowerCase();
 
                 if (landingPageType === "pages" || landingPageType === "blog") {
 
                     if (landingPageType === "blog") {
 
                         adConfig.pageTargeting["BlogId"] = "";
                     }
 
                     adConfig.pageTargeting["LandingPageType"] = [landingPageType];
                     adConfig.pageTargeting["LandingPage"] = ["default.aspx"];
                 }
             }
 
             //Code to send target parameters
             adConfig.pageTargeting["URL"] = window.location.href;
 
             //send the URL as a multiword value. 
             adConfig.pageTargeting["UrlSegments"] = adService.getUrlSegments();
 
             adConfig.pageTargeting["cid"] = "";
         }
 
         SetAdditionalTargetting();
 
         adService.displayAds(adConfig);
     }
     catch (e) {
         //console.log("Error : " + e.message);
     }
   </script>
